#Subterfuge Phase Internal Event Chain (000-049):
country_event = { #Crumbling Hegemonies in China
	id = GXC.introgame.001
	title = GXC.introgame.001.t
	desc = GXC.introgame.001.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_liu_zhilu

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by EVENT: league_collapse.1. #Sun Chuanfang meets with Governors // Fires Jan 05 1936

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = GXC.introgame.002 days = 7 } #Warring Factions in Eastern Guangdong
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.introgame.001 option GXC.introgame.001.a"
		name = GXC.introgame.001.a #Reinforce Liu Zhilu in Guilin in case Sun and Shen get any funny ideas.
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		599 = { GXC_introgame_NPA_add_state_strength_effect = yes } #Guilin
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.introgame.001 option GXC.introgame.001.b"
		name = GXC.introgame.001.b #Can we even trust General Liu to manage Guilin anymore?
		ai_chance = { base = 35 }
		599 = { GXC_introgame_KMT_add_state_strength_effect = yes } #Guilin
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.introgame.001 option GXC.introgame.001.c"
		name = GXC.introgame.001.c #Our tacit alliance with Governor Zhao of Hunan keeps Sun at bay.
		ai_chance = { base = 35 }
		599 = { GXC_introgame_UPC_add_state_strength_effect = yes } #Guilin
	}
}

country_event = { #Turning Point in Guangzhou
	id = GXC.introgame.010
	title = GXC.introgame.010.t
	desc = GXC.introgame.010.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_guangdong_guangzhou_troops_2

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [EVENT] GXC.introgame.010 #A War on Two Fronts // Fires March 1st 1936

	immediate = {
		#Mainly for ease of debugging
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_choose_KMT_side_flag }
			clr_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_choose_KMT_side_flag
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_choose_UPC_side_flag }
			clr_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_choose_UPC_side_flag
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_choose_NPA_side_flag }
			clr_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_choose_NPA_side_flag
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_KMT_eliminated_flag }
			clr_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_KMT_eliminated_flag
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_UPC_eliminated_flag }
			clr_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_UPC_eliminated_flag
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_NPA_eliminated_flag }
			clr_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_NPA_eliminated_flag
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.introgame.010 option GXC.introgame.010.a"
		name = GXC.introgame.010.a #Senator Chen Jiongming is named Governor by a divided assembly and a reluctant Mayor. [PLAY AS FEDERALISTS]
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			#Okay Quick Explainer about how GXC path odds will work.
			#As a base, odds are 35-30-35. (UPC-NPA-KMT).
			#For points of external help GXC gets, add weight (10 weight for 1-3 points, 20 weight for 4-6 points, 30 weight for 7+ points -> max a given side can get is 9)
			#If a tag took the decision to send additional support (only ai should never do), double the weight.
			#So maximum a singular tag can shift is 4 support points (YUN or HNN helping Feds), so 35+20 = 55, x2 makes it 110. 110/(110+35+30) = 62% chance of GXC going UPC, compared to baseline of 35%.

			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { GXC.GXC_UPC_introminigame_external_help_var > 6 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { GXC.GXC_UPC_introminigame_external_help_var > 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { GXC.GXC_UPC_introminigame_external_help_var > 0 }
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_flag = GXC_UPC_introminigame_reinforcements_flag
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_PATH option = GXC_PATH_NPA_AUTDEM }
					#has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_PATH option = GXC_PATH_UPC_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_PATH option = GXC_PATH_KMT_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC.introgame.010_UPC_tt
		592 = { GXC_introgame_UPC_add_state_strength_effect = yes } #Guangzhou
		set_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_choose_UPC_side_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = GXC_introminigame_KMT_make_their_move_mission
			activate_mission = GXC_introminigame_NPA_make_their_move_mission
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.introgame.010 option GXC.introgame.010.b"
		name = GXC.introgame.010.b #Mayor Chen Lianbo, seeing the assembly deadlocked, leaves to reassert control on his own. [PLAY AS REGIONALISTS]
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30

			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { GXC.GXC_NPA_introminigame_external_help_var > 6 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { GXC.GXC_NPA_introminigame_external_help_var > 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { GXC.GXC_NPA_introminigame_external_help_var > 0 }
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_introminigame_reinforcements_flag
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					#has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_PATH option = GXC_PATH_NPA_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_PATH option = GXC_PATH_UPC_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_PATH option = GXC_PATH_KMT_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC.introgame.010_NPA_tt
		592 = { GXC_introgame_NPA_add_state_strength_effect = yes } #Guangzhou
		set_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_choose_NPA_side_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = GXC_introminigame_KMT_make_their_move_mission
			activate_mission = GXC_introminigame_UPC_make_their_move_mission
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.introgame.010 option GXC.introgame.010.c"
		name = GXC.introgame.010.c #General Chen Jitang rapidly orchestrates an armed putsch amid stalled assembly negotiations. [PLAY AS NATIONALISTS]
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35

			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { GXC.GXC_KMT_introminigame_external_help_var > 6 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { GXC.GXC_KMT_introminigame_external_help_var > 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { GXC.GXC_KMT_introminigame_external_help_var > 0 }
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_flag = GXC_KMT_introminigame_reinforcements_flag
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_PATH option = GXC_PATH_NPA_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_PATH option = GXC_PATH_UPC_AUTDEM }
					#has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_PATH option = GXC_PATH_KMT_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC.introgame.010_KMT_tt
		592 = { GXC_introgame_KMT_add_state_strength_effect = yes } #Guangzhou
		set_country_flag = GXC_introminigame_choose_KMT_side_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = GXC_introminigame_UPC_make_their_move_mission
			activate_mission = GXC_introminigame_NPA_make_their_move_mission
		}
	}

	after = {
		activate_mission = GXC_frontlines_shift_in_liangguang_mission_timer
		set_variable = { GXC.GXC_introminigame_month_counter_var = 1 } #Reset the monthly counter variable to make debugging easier.
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = GXC.introgame.150 days = 1 } #Liangguang Devolves Into Civil War
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = GXC.liangguang_regions_array
				GXC = { activate_targeted_decision = { decision = GXC_introminigame_secure_state_decision target = PREV } }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Subterfuge Phase External Events (050-099):

country_event = { #Our Interests in Guangzhou
	id = GXC.introgame.050
	title = GXC.introgame.050.t
	desc = GXC.introgame.050.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_chen_lianbo_1

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [GXC History FIle] for JAP, FNG, LEC

	trigger = {
		GXC_is_phase_1_trigger = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.introgame.050 option GXC.introgame.050.a"
		name = GXC.introgame.050.a #The Mayor will receive a secret shipment of supplies.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10 #
			modifier = {
				tag = FNG
				factor = 2
			}
		}

		}
		GXC = { country_event = { id = GXC.introgame.051 days = 3 random_days = 4 } } #[FROM.GetNameDefCap] Supports Chen Lianbo
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.introgame.050 option GXC.introgame.050.b"
		name = GXC.introgame.050.b #The Mayor will receive a staunchly worded letter of support.

			base = 90 #
			modifier = {
				tag = FNG
				add = -10
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #X Forces Lose Momentum
	id = GXC.introgame.210
	title = {
		text = GXC.introgame.210.t.NPA #Regionalist Forces Lose Momentum
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_NPA_points_var < GXC.GXC_introgame_total_KMT_points_var }
			NOT = { check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_NPA_points_var > GXC.GXC_introgame_total_UPC_points_var } }
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = GXC.introgame.210.t.UPC #Federalist Forces Lose Momentum
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_UPC_points_var < GXC.GXC_introgame_total_NPA_points_var }
			NOT = { check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_UPC_points_var > GXC.GXC_introgame_total_KMT_points_var } }
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = GXC.introgame.210.t.KMT #Kuomintang Forces Lose Momentum
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_KMT_points_var < GXC.GXC_introgame_total_UPC_points_var }
					NOT = { check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_KMT_points_var > GXC.GXC_introgame_total_NPA_points_var } }
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_KMT_points_var = GXC.GXC_introgame_total_UPC_points_var }
					check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_UPC_points_var = GXC.GXC_introgame_total_NPA_points_var }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = GXC.introgame.210.d.NPA
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_NPA_points_var < GXC.GXC_introgame_total_KMT_points_var }
			NOT = { check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_NPA_points_var > GXC.GXC_introgame_total_UPC_points_var } }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.introgame.210.d.UPC
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_UPC_points_var < GXC.GXC_introgame_total_NPA_points_var }
			NOT = { check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_UPC_points_var > GXC.GXC_introgame_total_KMT_points_var } }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.introgame.210.d.KMT
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_KMT_points_var < GXC.GXC_introgame_total_UPC_points_var }
					NOT = { check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_KMT_points_var > GXC.GXC_introgame_total_NPA_points_var } }
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_KMT_points_var = GXC.GXC_introgame_total_UPC_points_var }
					check_variable = { GXC.GXC_introgame_total_UPC_points_var = GXC.GXC_introgame_total_NPA_points_var }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_China_soldier_retreating

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [DECISION] GXC_frontlines_shift_in_liangguang_mission_timer
	trigger = {
		GXC_is_phase_1_trigger = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.introgame.210 option GXC.introgame.210.a"
		name = GXC.introgame.210.a #One foe down, another to go.
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_war_support = -0.10
		GXC_introgame_eliminate_the_weakest_faction_scripted_effect = yes
	}
}

		GXC_zhang_gan = { custom_effect_tooltip = character_becomes_a_general }
		GXC_yang_chisheng = { custom_effect_tooltip = character_becomes_a_general }
		GXC_yang_ruxuan = { custom_effect_tooltip = character_becomes_a_general }

			limit = { china_is_aligned_with_right_kmt = yes }
			GXC_NGX_medium_effect = yes
			RKT_sub_zeal_medium_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_is_aligned_with_left_kmt = yes }
			GXC_PPP_small_effect = yes
			GXC_NGX_large_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_is_aligned_with_federalists = yes }
			GXC_SAF_large_effect = yes
			GXC_YUE_small_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC_zhang_gan = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			GXC_yang_chisheng = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			GXC_yang_ruxuan = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.earlygame.001 option GXC.earlygame.001.b"

		ai_chance = { base = 100 }

		}

			limit = { china_is_aligned_with_left_kmt = yes }

		}

		}

		name = GXC.earlygame.032.a #Semi-motorization
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Motuo Hua" } }
			division_template = {
				name = "Motuo Hua"

					cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }

					motorized = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					motorized = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = tooltip_create_division_template
				NAME = "Motuo Hua"
				LINE_1 = { localization_key = line_battalion_tt NAME = cavalry ICON = GFX_unit_cavalry_icon_small COUNT = 2 }
				LINE_2 = { localization_key = line_battalion_tt NAME = motorized ICON = GFX_unit_motorized_icon_small COUNT = 2 }
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 592 }
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				is_in_home_area = yes
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Motuo Hua\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
				owner = ROOT
				count = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.earlygame.032 option GXC.earlygame.032.b"
		name = GXC.earlygame.032.b #Cavalry First
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Qibing Xie" } }
			division_template = {
				name = "Qibing Xie" #Cavalry
				division_names_group = "GXC_CAV_01"
				regiments = {
					cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = tooltip_create_division_template
				NAME = "Qibing Xie"
				LINE_1 = { localization_key = line_battalion_tt NAME = cavalry ICON = GFX_unit_cavalry_icon_small COUNT = 4 }

		}

			producer = GER
		}

		}
	}
	option = {

			NOT = { has_war_with = JAP }

		}

		}
	}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_war_with = IMP }
				NOT = { has_war_with = 361.owner } #Maryland
			}
		}

			limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = 361.owner } }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = 1000
				producer = USA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = IMP } }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = 1000
				producer = IMP
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { china_is_aligned_with_federalists = yes }
			GXC_DSP_medium_effect = yes
			GXC_CMC_medium_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_is_aligned_with_kmt = yes }
			GXC_RCF_large_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			GXC_PIP_medium_effect = yes
			GXC_PSC_medium_effect = yes
		}
	}
	option = {

		name = GXC.earlygame.041.e #Domestic
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = GXC_secure_foreign_benefactors
			bonus = 0.75
			uses = 2
			category = industry
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Rice Glut
	id = GXC.earlygame.200
	title = GXC.earlygame.200.t
	desc = GXC.earlygame.200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_expensive_rice

	is_triggered_only = yes #Agrarian Stabilisation timer
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.earlygame.200 option GXC.earlygame.200.a"
		name = GXC.earlygame.200.a #We must grease the wheels of progress!
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		add_political_power = -30
		if = {
			limit = { china_is_aligned_with_kmt = yes }
			GXC_NGX_medium_effect = yes
			GXC_GFA_medium_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_is_aligned_with_federalists = yes }
			GXC_SAF_large_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			GXC_SAF_medium_effect = yes
			GXC_CMC_medium_effect = yes
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = { has_state_flag = guangxi_province_state }
			prioritize = { 594 599 } #Nanning, Guilin
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.earlygame.200 option GXC.earlygame.200.b"
		name = GXC.earlygame.200.b #Change is coming, but we must conserve our political capital.
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		add_political_power = 15
		if = {
			limit = { china_is_aligned_with_kmt = yes }
			GXC_WHC_large_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_is_aligned_with_federalists = yes }
			GXC_PIP_small_effect = yes
			GXC_DSP_small_effect = yes
			GXC_GIM_medium_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			GXC_YGF_medium_effect = yes
			GXC_CMC_medium_effect = yes
		}
	}
	after = {
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GXC_agricultural_reform_idea2
			add_idea = GXC_agricultural_reform_idea3
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_agricultural_tree_available_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { #Failsafe
				limit = { has_active_mission = GXC_agricultural_stabilisation_mission_timer }
				remove_mission = GXC_agricultural_stabilisation_mission_timer
			}
		}
	}
}

###KMT Political Event Chain (400-429)
country_event = {
	id = GXC.earlygame.400
	title = GXC.earlygame.400.t
	desc = GXC.earlygame.400.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_successful_northern_expedition_flag

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes #Essential so you can't double up somehow.

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC = { country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.402 days = 3 } } #Tensions in Guangdong
			CHI = { country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.460 days = 7 } } #The Clash for Canton
			every_army_leader = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = CHN_yue_clique_officer_trait
					has_character_flag = GXC_NGD_character_flag
				}
				remove_trait = { trait = CHN_yue_clique_officer_trait }
				add_trait = { trait = CHN_RKT_officer_trait }
			}

			log = "KR_Event_Logging;GXC GAME PROGRESS - GXC KMT Other"
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.earlygame.400 option GXC.earlygame.400.a"
		name = GXC.earlygame.400.a
		hidden_effect = {
			#New Fourth Army
			GXC_chen_mingshu = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			GXC_cai_tingkai = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			GXC_jiang_guangnai = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			#New Guangxi
			GXC_li_zongren = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			GXC_bai_chongxi = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			GXC_huang_shaohong = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			#New Guangdong
			GXC_chen_jitang = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			GXC_fan_hanjie = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			GXC_chen_weizhou = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			#RCF
			GXC_liang_hancao = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			GXC_chen_ce = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			set_country_flag = GXC_phase_2_begins_flag
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			GXC_KMT_set_initial_parties = yes
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = GXC_EDC_character_flag
					has_character_flag = GXC_NGD_character_flag
					has_character_flag = GXC_NGX_character_flag
					has_character_flag = GXC_WHC_character_flag
					has_character_flag = GXC_RCF_character_flag
					has_character_flag = GXC_PPP_character_flag
					has_character_flag = GXC_GFA_character_flag
					has_character_flag = GXC_GPA_character_flag
					has_character_flag = GXC_SPO_character_flag
					has_character_flag = GXC_SPR_character_flag
					is_character = GXC_assorted_leaders
					is_character = GXC_ding_jixu
				}
			}
			retire = yes
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			promote_character = {
				character = GXC_chen_jitang
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
		}
		activate_advisor = GXC_li_zongren_sic
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GXC_shared_popular_support_0
			add_idea = GXC_KMT_popular_support_1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = focus_tree_will_change_tt
		complete_national_focus = GXC_cradle_of_the_national_revolution
		GXC = {
			set_capital = { state = 592 remember_old_capital = no } #Guangzhou
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = GXC_KMT
			#Promote the Junta to Field Marshal Roles
			GXC_li_zongren = { promote_to_field_marshal = yes }
			GXC_chen_mingshu = { promote_to_field_marshal = yes }
			GXC_chen_jitang = { promote_to_field_marshal = yes }
			news_event = GXC.earlygame.401
		}
	}
}

###KMT Clash for Canton Related Events (460-499)
country_event = {
	id = GXC.earlygame.460 #The Clash for Canton Begins
	title = GXC.earlygame.460.t
	desc = GXC.earlygame.460.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_successful_northern_expedition_flag

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by GXC.earlygame.400, informs CHI that Clash for Canton is Beginning.

	trigger = {
		GXC = { NOT = { is_ally_with = CHI } }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.earlygame.460 option GXC.earlygame.460.a"
		name = GXC.earlygame.460.a #We must prevail! Deploy reinforcements!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_completed_focus = CHI_deal_with_warlords
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		GXC = {
			random_list = {
				25 = { country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.465 days = 3 } } #Peasants Organising in the Countryside
				25 = { country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.466 days = 3 } } #Syndicalist Agitation in Canton
				25 = { country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.467 days = 3 } } #Republican Intellectuals Protest
				25 = { country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.468 days = 3 } } #Fourth Army Reinforcements
			}
		}
		GXC = { set_country_flag = GXC_LKMT_aggressive_AI_strategy_flag } #If LKMT decided to go aggressive, GXC will help you out.
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.earlygame.460 option GXC.earlygame.460.b"
		name = GXC.earlygame.460.b #General Chen can get a handle on things...
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = china_is_potential_government #If League war is over, less likely to select this option
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_forpol option = GXC_FORPOL_LKMT }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = GXC.earlygame.462 #New Fourth Army Coup
	title = GXC.earlygame.462.t
	desc = {
		text = GXC.earlygame.462.d.CHI_initated
		trigger = { FROM = { tag = CHI } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.earlygame.462.d.GXC_initated
		trigger = { FROM = { tag = GXC } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_successful_northern_expedition_flag

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by decisions GXC_execute_leftist_coup_decision and GXC_CHI_order_chen_mingshu_forward. Also china_puppet_ROOT_effect if you have game rules.

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.earlygame.462 option GXC.earlygame.462.a"
		name = GXC.earlygame.462.a #Li Marches Out!
		trigger = {
			FROM = { tag = CHI }
			NOT = {
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_RADSOC }
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_RADSOC }
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_SOCDEM }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_country_flag = china_refused_alliance_@FROM
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { china_possible_allies_array = FROM } }
			remove_from_array = { china_possible_allies_array = FROM }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { china_possible_allies_array_northwest = FROM } }
			remove_from_array = { china_possible_allies_array_northwest = FROM }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = { country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.463 days = 1 } } #Chen Mingshu's Coup Fails
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_soc_dem_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@social_democrat }
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_rad_soc_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_syndie_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@syndicalist }

		#GXC loses half of each leftist ideology (minus totalists who are irrelevant
		divide_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_soc_dem_temp_var = -2 }
		divide_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_rad_soc_temp_var = -2 }
		divide_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_syndie_temp_var = -2 }

		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = GXC_CHI_coup_soc_dem_temp_var }
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = GXC_CHI_coup_rad_soc_temp_var }
		add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = GXC_CHI_coup_syndie_temp_var }

		GXC_NGX_giga_effect = yes #Li Zongren doesn't become countryleader but does get compensated handsomely

		#GXC loses war support equivalent to loss of Rad Soc (Peasant) popularity, stability equivalent to Syndicalist (Union) popularity, and tanks both equivalent to half of Soc Dem (army) popularity
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_war_support_loss = GXC_CHI_coup_rad_soc_temp_var }
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_stability_loss = GXC_CHI_coup_syndie_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_war_support_loss = 2 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_stability_loss = 2 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_war_support_loss = GXC_CHI_coup_soc_dem_temp_var }
		add_to_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_stability_loss = GXC_CHI_coup_soc_dem_temp_var }
		add_war_support = GXC_CHI_coup_war_support_loss
		add_stability = GXC_CHI_coup_stability_loss
		effect_tooltip = {
			800 = { transfer_state_to = CHI } #Shaoguan
			1012 = { transfer_state_to = CHI } #Huiyang
			592 = { transfer_state_to = CHI } #Guangzhou
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = may_lead_to_war_with
			COUNTRY = "[CHI.GetNameDef]"
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.earlygame.462 option GXC.earlygame.462.b"
		name = GXC.earlygame.462.b #Li Submits to Reality.
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = { country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.464 days = 1 } } #Chen Mingshu's Coup Succeeds
			GXC = { country_event = { id = GXC.midgame.540 days = 14 } } #The Organic Law of Guangdong
		}
		#GXC loses stability, war support, and political power proportionate to auth dem popularity.
		set_country_flag = GXC_LKMT_satellite_narrative_flag
		complete_national_focus = GXC_a_red_liangguang
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		set_politics = { ruling_party = social_democrat }
		promote_character = {
			character = GXC_chen_mingshu
			ideology = social_democrat_subtype
		}
		activate_advisor = GXC_li_zongren_sic
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_auth_dem_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
		divide_temp_variable = { GXC_CHI_coup_auth_dem_temp_var = -2 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = GXC_CHI_coup_auth_dem_temp_var }
		add_war_support = GXC_CHI_coup_auth_dem_temp_var
		add_stability = GXC_CHI_coup_auth_dem_temp_var
		GXC_NGD_purge_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI = { china_puppet_ROOT_effect = yes }
		set_country_flag = GXC_phase_3_begins_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = GXC_BEI_character_flag
						has_character_flag = GXC_GIM_character_flag
						has_character_flag = GXC_CMC_character_flag
						has_character_flag = GXC_SAF_character_flag
						has_character_flag = GXC_YGF_character_flag
						has_character_flag = GXC_YUE_character_flag
						has_character_flag = GXC_DSP_character_flag
					}
					NOT = {
						is_character = GXC_ding_ying
						is_character = GXC_li_qingwen
						is_character = GXC_zhou_tianlu
					}
				}
				retire = yes
			}
		}
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;GXC GAME PROGRESS - GXC KMT Submit to LKT"
	}
}

			}

	desc = GXC.earlygame.800.d

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.801 days = 1 } #Regionalist Powers Hold Onto Liangguang
			country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.802 days = 3 } #North and South // Only 3 days because we need to explain the mechanic ASAP
			GXC = {
				activate_advisor = GXC_ma_ji_sic
				GXC_lu_yuguang = { promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
				#No need to change most stuff like 400 and 600 because NPA should be default.
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.earlygame.800 option GXC.earlygame.800.a"
		name = GXC.earlygame.800.a #The way things were, but not quite what it ought to be.

			remove_idea = GXC_shared_popular_support_0

		}
		set_country_flag = GXC_phase_2_begins_flag

		complete_national_focus = GXC_heirs_of_lu_rongting
		custom_effect_tooltip = focus_tree_will_change_tt

		log = "KR_Event_Logging;GXC GAME PROGRESS - GXC NPA Other"
	}
}

### NPA Southern Struggle Mini-Game Events (860-889):
country_event = {
	id = GXC.earlygame.860 #The Southern Struggle Begins
	title = GXC.earlygame.860.t
	desc = GXC.earlygame.860.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_successful_northern_expedition_flag

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by GXC.earlygame.400, informs FNG/QIE/LEP/ANQ/SHD that Clash for Canton is Beginning.

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.earlygame.860 option GXC.earlygame.860.a"
		name = GXC.earlygame.860.a #We must prevail! Redouble our efforts!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				china_is_potential_government = yes
				has_war = no
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		GXC = {
			random_list = {
				20 = { country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.861 days = 3 } } #[FROM.Adjective] Aid and Praise
				20 = { country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.862 days = 3 } } #Reports of Bribery by [FROM.Adjective] Agents
				#These events make no sense if you're disconnected so only going to limit these to the LEP trio that can actually get these events normally
				20 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = {
							tag = LEP #Nanjing
							tag = ANQ #Nanjing
							tag = SHD #Nanjing
						}
					}
					country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.863 days = 3 } #Military Threats from [FROM.GetNameDefCap]
				}
				20 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = {
							tag = LEP #Nanjing
							tag = ANQ #Nanjing
							tag = SHD #Nanjing
						}
					}
					country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.864 days = 3 } #[FROM.GetNameDefCap] Accommodates Local Warlords
				}
				20 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = {
							tag = LEP #Nanjing
							tag = ANQ #Nanjing
							tag = SHD #Nanjing
						}
					}
					country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.865 days = 3 } #[FROM.GetNameDefCap] Offers Peace Feelers
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					china_alignment_northern_zhili = yes
					china_alignment_southern_zhili = yes
				}
			}
			GXC = { set_country_flag = GXC_Zhili_aggressive_AI_strategy_flag } #If Zhili decided to go aggressive, GXC will help you out.
		}
		else = {
			GXC = { set_country_flag = GXC_Fengtian_aggressive_AI_strategy_flag }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.earlygame.860 option GXC.earlygame.860.b"
		name = GXC.earlygame.860.b #Hopefully they will align on their own...
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				#AI League winner will try to align GXC first if possible because they have an advantage in doing so
				china_is_potential_government = yes
				OR = {
					tag = LEP
					tag = ANQ
					tag = SHD
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					}

		}

				china_autonomy_level_down = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = GXC.midgame.507 #Showdown in the Central Committee
	title = GXC.midgame.507.t
	desc = {
		text = GXC.midgame.507.d_sun
		trigger = { has_character = CHI_sun_fo }
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.midgame.507.d_nosun
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character = CHI_sun_fo } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_hu_hanmin_speech_2

	is_triggered_only = yes #triggered by event: GXC.midgame.506

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.midgame.507 option GXC.midgame.507.a"
		name = GXC.midgame.507.a #Hu motions for a closed vote by the Central Executive Committee.
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		#Guarantees the same outcome - every time.

		#Rig outcome if you have game rules
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_HANMIN_PRINCIPLED_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_HANMIN_REVOLUTIONARY_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_game_rule_rigged_warning_tt
			country_event = { id = GXC.midgame.508 days = 3 } #The Chairman Prevails! - Unlocks the high zeal ending
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_HANMIN_DIARCHY_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_PATAUT }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_game_rule_rigged_warning_tt
			country_event = { id = GXC.midgame.509 days = 3 } #The Chairman Falls! - Unlocks low zeal ending
		}
		#Normal way this works
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { global.RKT_revolutionary_zeal_var < 0.65 } }
			}
			country_event = { id = GXC.midgame.508 days = 3 } #The Chairman Prevails! - Unlocks the high zeal ending
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = GXC.midgame.509 days = 3 } #The Chairman Falls! - Unlocks low zeal ending
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_RKMT_showdown_closed_tt
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.midgame.507 option GXC.midgame.507.b"
		name = GXC.midgame.507.b #Hu moves for a public vote by the Kuomintang National Party Congress.
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		#Random, weighted outcome
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				seed = global.date #Allows for save scumming.
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						#Our goal here is to multiply the chance of winning by amount of Zeal % above 50%.
						#So at 100%, the chance of winning increases by 50% (aka 75 total points).
						#At 0%, the chance of winning decreases by 50% (aka 25 total points).
						set_temp_variable = { GXC_hu_hanmin_win_bonus_temp_var = global.RKT_revolutionary_zeal_var } #Zeal is always between 0-1.
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_hu_hanmin_win_bonus_temp_var = 0.5 } #We are subtracting 0.5 from it. So the result will be between -0.5 to 0.5.
						add_to_temp_variable = { GXC_hu_hanmin_win_bonus_temp_var = 1 } #Now we are adding 1, so it'll range between 0.5-1.5
						factor = GXC_hu_hanmin_win_bonus_temp_var
					}
					country_event = { id = GXC.midgame.508 days = 3 } #The Chairman Prevails! - Unlocks the high zeal ending
				}
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						#Our goal here is to multiply the chance of winning by amount of Zeal % below 50%.
						#So at 100%, the chance of winning decreases by 50% (aka 25 total points).
						#At 0%, the chance of winning increases by 50% (aka 75 total points).
						set_temp_variable = { GXC_li_zongren_win_bonus_temp_var = global.RKT_revolutionary_zeal_var } #Zeal is always between 0-1.
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_li_zongren_win_bonus_temp_var = 0.5 } #We are subtracting 0.5 from it. So the result will be between -0.5 to 0.5.
						multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_li_zongren_win_bonus_temp_var = -1 } #So now it all inverses, -0.5 becomes 0.5 and vice versa. So 0.5 to -0.5
						add_to_temp_variable = { GXC_li_zongren_win_bonus_temp_var = 1 } #Now we are adding 1, so it'll range between 1.5-0.5
						factor = GXC_li_zongren_win_bonus_temp_var
					}
					country_event = { id = GXC.midgame.509 days = 3 } #The Chairman Falls! - Unlocks low zeal ending
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_RKMT_showdown_open_tt
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = GXC.midgame.508 #The Chairman Prevails!
	title = GXC.midgame.508.t
	desc = GXC.midgame.508.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_hu_hanmin_15

	is_triggered_only = yes #triggered by event: GXC.midgame.507

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GXC_phase_4_begins_flag
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.400 days = 170 random_days = 20 } #The Divisions of 1911
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_or_potential_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = GXC.midgame.513 days = 1 } #Hu Hanmin Prevails
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.midgame.508 option GXC.midgame.508.a"
		name = GXC.midgame.508.a #Li can enjoy commanding the kitchen staff.
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_political_power = -50
		add_command_power = -50
		if = {
			limit = { GXC_li_zongren = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			activate_advisor = GXC_li_wenfan_sic
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.midgame.508 option GXC.midgame.508.b"
		name = GXC.midgame.508.b #Hope they enjoy time abroad and learn a lot!
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		if = { #Needs to be done before retiring Li
			limit = { GXC_li_zongren = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			activate_advisor = GXC_li_wenfan_sic
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		retire_character = GXC_li_zongren
		retire_character = GXC_bai_chongxi
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = GXC_huang_xuchu }
			retire_character = GXC_huang_xuchu
		}
		promote_character = {
			character = GXC_huang_shaohong
			ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = -0.10 }
	}

	after = {
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = GXC_man_of_principle_tt #Why not just use vanilla tooltip for country leader trait addition?
			GXC_hu_hanmin = { add_trait = { trait = GXC_man_of_principle ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype } }
		}
	}
}

	###########################################################

	####- Chiang Kai-shrek Dev Note for Future Maintenance -###
	###########################################################
	###########################################################
	#The chain here is meant to be good for collaborative play - the CHI player signals in GXC.midgame.542 their preference for GXC, and GXC then makes their own decision in GXC.midgame.543 (rewarded if they follow)
	#GXC's choices basically split as follows:
	#Sending troops out will create an internal event chain that will ultimately decide GXC's winner (and the potential CHI challenger) by greatest popularity.
	#GXC keeping troops home sends an event to CHI letting them pick GXC's winner by spending political power proportionate to GXC's existing party popularity
	#Fighting will weaken both, working together will ensure careful distribution of resources.
	#For singeplayer, Chen Mingshu is the best outcome for CHI because he will be the least likely to revolt. CHI can maximize its chance for a positive outcome by giving ambiguous orders, and then appointing Chen.

	option = {

		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_LKMT_Chen_ordered_to_act_tt
		GXC = { save_event_target_as = GXC_Chen_ordered_to_act }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.midgame.542 option GXC.midgame.542.b"
		name = GXC.midgame.542.b #Make a terse statement calling for calm.
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		add_political_power = -50
		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_LKMT_Chen_ordered_to_calm_tt
	}

	after = {

			GXC = { country_event = { id = GXC.midgame.543 days = 1 } } #A Statement from [CHI.Capital.GetCapitalVictoryPointName]
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = GXC.midgame.547 #The War Council at Nanning
	title = GXC.midgame.547.t
	desc = GXC.midgame.547.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_chen_mingshu_2

	is_triggered_only = yes #triggered by EVENT: GXC.midgame.546
	timeout_days = 7 #Quick-time event because we need this chain resolved relatively fast.

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.midgame.547 option GXC.midgame.547.a"
		name = GXC.midgame.547.a #The deal is accepted.
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }

		add_command_power = -100

		#Add Soc Dem Party Popularity = to Soc Lib and Pat Aut Combined
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_PPP_bonus_from_rightists_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@social_liberal } #0-1
		add_to_temp_variable = { GXC_PPP_bonus_from_rightists_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat } #0.2
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = GXC_PPP_bonus_from_rightists_temp_var }

		#Subtract Rad Soc Popularity = to Pat Aut
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_rad_soc_loss_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat } #0-1
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_rad_soc_loss_temp_var = -1 } #-1-0
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = GXC_rad_soc_loss_temp_var }

		#Subtract Syndie Popularity = Soc Lib
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_syndie_loss_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@syndicalist } #0-1
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_syndie_loss_temp_var = -1 } #-1-0
		add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = GXC_syndie_loss_temp_var }

		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_LKMT_chen_mingshu_deal_with_rightist_tt
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.midgame.547 option GXC.midgame.547.b"
		name = GXC.midgame.547.b #We do not need them.
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }

		#Token bonus for doing the right thing *Condescending Headpat*
		GXC_PPP_small_effect = yes

		#Remove Soc Lib popularity - add it to Syndicalists
		add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = ROOT.party_popularity@social_liberal }
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_soc_lib_loss_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@social_liberal } #0-1
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_soc_lib_loss_temp_var = -1 } #-1-0
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = GXC_soc_lib_loss_temp_var }

		#Remove Pat Aut popularity - add it to Rad Soc
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = ROOT.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_pat_aut_loss_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat } #0-1
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_pat_aut_loss_temp_var = -1 } #-1-0
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = GXC_pat_aut_loss_temp_var }

		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_LKMT_chen_mingshu_no_deal_with_rightist_tt

		GXC_NGX_purge_advisors_effect = yes
		GXC_RCF_purge_advisors_effect = yes
		activate_advisor = GXC_jiang_guangnai_sic
	}

	after = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_game_rule_rigged_warning_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC_LKMT_decide_phase_iv_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

		GXC_NGX_purge_advisors_effect = yes
	}

		CHI_LCS_medium_effect = yes

country_event = {
	id = GXC.midgame.552 #The Cantonese Quarrel
	title = GXC.midgame.552.t
	desc = GXC.midgame.552.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_chen_mingshu_speech
	is_triggered_only = yes #triggered by GXC EVENT: GXC.midgame.551
	timeout_days = 7 #Quick-time event because we need this chain resolved relatively fast.

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.midgame.552 option GXC.midgame.552.a"
		name = GXC.midgame.552.a #Tan Pingshan will take over his duties
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				check_variable = { GXC.party_popularity@syndicalist > GXC.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
				check_variable = { GXC.party_popularity@syndicalist > GXC.party_popularity@social_democrat }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					#has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_SOCDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		#For every non-Syndicalist party popularity in GXC, costs 1pp (max 100).
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = GXC.party_popularity@syndicalist }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = -100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = CHN_deduct_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_in_country_tt
			IDEOLOGY = syndicalist_coloured COUNTRY = "[GXC.GetNameDef]"
		}
		add_political_power = GXC_pp_loss_temp_var
		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_LKMT_CHI_tan_pingshan_warning_tt

		hidden_effect = { GXC = { country_event = { id = GXC.midgame.553 days = 1 } } } #Tan Pingshan is Appointed Governor
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.midgame.552 option GXC.midgame.552.b"
		name = GXC.midgame.552.b #Peng Pai is a dark horse candidate.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				check_variable = { GXC.party_popularity@radical_socialist > GXC.party_popularity@syndicalist }
				check_variable = { GXC.party_popularity@radical_socialist > GXC.party_popularity@social_democrat }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_RADSOC }
					#has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_SOCDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		#For every non-Rad Soc party popularity in GXC, costs 1pp (max 100).
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = GXC.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = -100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = CHN_deduct_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_in_country_tt
			IDEOLOGY = radical_socialist_coloured COUNTRY = "[GXC.GetNameDef]"
		}
		add_political_power = GXC_pp_loss_temp_var
		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_LKMT_CHI_peng_pai_warning_tt

		hidden_effect = { GXC = { country_event = { id = GXC.midgame.554 days = 1 } } } #Peng Pai, the Dark Horse Candidate
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.midgame.552 option GXC.midgame.552.c"
		name = GXC.midgame.552.c #Chen Mingshu will remain in place.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				check_variable = { GXC.party_popularity@social_democrat > GXC.party_popularity@syndicalist }
				check_variable = { GXC.party_popularity@social_democrat > GXC.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_RADSOC }
					#has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_SOCDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		#For every non-Soc Dem party popularity in GXC, costs 1pp (max 100).
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = GXC.party_popularity@social_democrat }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = -100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = CHN_deduct_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_in_country_tt
			IDEOLOGY = social_democrat_coloured COUNTRY = "[GXC.GetNameDef]"
		}
		add_political_power = GXC_pp_loss_temp_var
		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_LKMT_CHI_chen_mingshu_warning_tt

		hidden_effect = { GXC = { country_event = { id = GXC.midgame.555 days = 1 } } } #Chen Mingshu Confirmed As Governor
	}

		trigger = {

					china_alignment_northern_zhili = yes

				china_alignment_geacps = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		GXC = { GXC_YGF_large_effect = yes }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.midgame.860 option GXC.midgame.860.b"
		name = GXC.midgame.860.b #Marshal Lu eyes Governor Shen warily.
		trigger = {
			var:GXC.overlord = {
				OR = {
					china_alignment_northern_zhili = yes
					china_alignment_southern_zhili = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		GXC = {
			GXC_SAF_mega_effect = yes
			set_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.midgame.860 option GXC.midgame.860.c"
		name = GXC.midgame.860.c #Marshal Lu eyes Mayor Chen warily.
		trigger = {
			var:GXC.overlord = {
				OR = {
					china_alignment_fengtian = yes

				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		GXC = {
			GXC_CMC_mega_effect = yes
			set_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_chen_lianbo_favored_flag
		}
	}

	after = {
		GXC = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_narrative_flag } }
				set_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_narrative_flag
				complete_national_focus = GXC_the_south_submits
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #The Democratic Awakening
	id = GXC.lategame.434
	title = GXC.lategame.434.t
	desc = GXC.lategame.434.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_1948_presidential_election

	is_triggered_only = yes #Event: GXC.lategame.433

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_or_potential_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.444 days = 3 random_days = 4 } #A Party Democracy?
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.434 option GXC.lategame.434.a"
		name = GXC.lategame.434.a #Hu Hanmin secures another term.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				check_variable = { party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat > party_popularity@social_liberal }
				check_variable = { party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat > party_popularity@social_conservative }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_SOCCON }
					#has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_HANMIN_PRINCIPLED_AUTDEM }
					#has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_HANMIN_REVOLUTIONARY_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		#Lose political power and stability proportionate to difference between party popularity and 100%
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat } #Between 0-1

		set_temp_variable = { GXC_stability_loss_temp_var = GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_stability_loss_temp_var = -0.25 } #Between -0.25 to 0.00
		add_stability = GXC_stability_loss_temp_var

		set_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = -200 } #Between -200 to 0.00
		add_political_power = GXC_pp_loss_temp_var

		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = CHN_deduct_stab_and_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_tt
			IDEOLOGY = authoritarian_democrat_coloured
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.441 days = 1 } #A New Mandate for an Old Chairman
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.434 option GXC.lategame.434.b"
		name = GXC.lategame.434.b #Ju Zheng gains his mandate.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				check_variable = { party_popularity@social_conservative > party_popularity@social_liberal }
				check_variable = { party_popularity@social_conservative > party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_SOCLIB }
					#has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_HANMIN_PRINCIPLED_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_HANMIN_REVOLUTIONARY_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		#Lose political power and stability proportionate to difference between party popularity and 100%
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var = party_popularity@social_conservative } #Between 0-1

		set_temp_variable = { GXC_stability_loss_temp_var = GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_stability_loss_temp_var = -0.25 } #Between -0.25 to 0.00
		add_stability = GXC_stability_loss_temp_var

		set_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = -200 } #Between -200 to 0.00
		add_political_power = GXC_pp_loss_temp_var

		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = CHN_deduct_stab_and_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_tt
			IDEOLOGY = social_conservative_coloured
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.442 days = 1 } #Ju Zheng wins the vote
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.434 option GXC.lategame.434.c"
		name = GXC.lategame.434.c #Sun Fo orchestrates an upset.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				check_variable = { party_popularity@social_liberal > party_popularity@social_conservative }
				check_variable = { party_popularity@social_liberal > party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					#has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_HANMIN_PRINCIPLED_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_HANMIN_REVOLUTIONARY_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		#Lose political power and stability proportionate to difference between party popularity and 100%
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var = party_popularity@social_liberal } #Between 0-1

		set_temp_variable = { GXC_stability_loss_temp_var = GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_stability_loss_temp_var = -0.25 } #Between -0.25 to 0.00
		add_stability = GXC_stability_loss_temp_var

		set_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = -200 } #Between -200 to 0.00
		add_political_power = GXC_pp_loss_temp_var

		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = CHN_deduct_stab_and_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_tt
			IDEOLOGY = social_liberal_coloured
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.443 days = 1 } #Sun Fo the Dark Horse Victor
		}
	}

			}

	}
	desc = {

	is_triggered_only = yes #Event: GXC.lategame.434.c

		trigger = {
			CHN_has_civil_war_prep_trigger = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {

				}
			}
			modifier = {

					ratio > 0.8
				}

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_chinese_tag = no
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GXC
					ratio < 0.75
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				check_variable = { CHN_civil_war_preparation_var > 0 }
			}
		}

		#Penalty depending on your alignment - PP and Stab already deducted earlier.
		if = {
			limit = { china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes } #PREV is GXC
			add_command_power = -100
			add_war_support = -0.10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes } #LKMT or Republicans
			add_command_power = -50
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			#Everyone else
			add_command_power = -30
			add_war_support = -0.03
		}

		#Break the Puppetship
		china_break_puppet_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FROM
				type = topple_government
			}
		}

		#Inform GXC
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = YUN }
				country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.550 days = 0 } #Advance of the National Protectors

			every_other_country = {

			}
		}
	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.444 option GXC.lategame.444.b"
		name = GXC.lategame.444.b #Congratulations to Chairman [GXC.GetLeader].

	title = GXC.lategame.445.t
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.445.d.yunkmt
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = YUN
				china_alignment_right_kuomintang = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.445.d.shxgmj
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = SHX
				has_country_leader = {
					character = SHX_feng_yuxiang
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.445.d.shxyan
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = SHX
				has_country_leader = {
					character = SHX_yan_xishan
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.445.d.generic
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					tag = SHX
					AND = {
						tag = YUN
						china_alignment_right_kuomintang = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_NRA_soldiers_3

	is_triggered_only = yes #Event: GXC.lategame.444.a, GXC.lategame.515.a, GXC.lategame.516.a

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.445 option GXC.lategame.445.a"
		name = GXC.lategame.445.a #We will put those traitors to shame!
		trigger = { tag = GXC }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FROM
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.445 option GXC.lategame.445.b"
		name = GXC.lategame.445.b #An unfathomable betrayal!
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = GXC } }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Faceoff in [ROOT.Capital.GetCapitalVictoryPointName]
	id = GXC.lategame.504
	title = GXC.lategame.504.t
	desc = GXC.lategame.504.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_hu_hanmin_dinner

	is_triggered_only = yes #FOCUS: GXC_complete_the_revolutionary_mission

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.504 option GXC.lategame.504.a"
		name = GXC.lategame.504.a #Li Zongren and his diverse allies have won the race.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				check_variable = { GXC.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat > GXC.party_popularity@social_conservative }
			}
		}
		#Lose political power and stability proportionate to difference between party popularity and 100%
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var = party_popularity@paternal_autocrat } #Between 0-1

		set_temp_variable = { GXC_stability_loss_temp_var = GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_stability_loss_temp_var = -0.25 } #Between -0.25 to 0.00
		add_stability = GXC_stability_loss_temp_var

		set_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = -200 } #Between -200 to 0.00
		add_political_power = GXC_pp_loss_temp_var

		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = CHN_deduct_stab_and_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_tt
			IDEOLOGY = paternal_autocrat_coloured
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			#Rig it if you have game rules
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_HANMIN_DIARCHY_AUTDEM }
				}
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.512 days = 14 } #New Guangdong Overthrows the Government
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_PATAUT }
				}
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.511 days = 14 } #New Guangxi Smashes the Opposition
			}
			#Normal Pathing
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat > party_popularity@paternal_autocrat } }
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.512 days = 14 } #New Guangdong Overthrows the Government
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.511 days = 14 } #New Guangxi Smashes the Opposition
			}
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_or_potential_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.515 days = 1 random_days = 2 } #The Republic Teeters to the Brink
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.504 option GXC.lategame.504.b"
		name = GXC.lategame.504.b #Ju Zheng and the establishment has secured an upset.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				check_variable = { GXC.party_popularity@social_conservative > GXC.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		#Lose political power and stability proportionate to difference between party popularity and 100%
		set_temp_variable = { GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var = party_popularity@social_conservative } #Between 0-1

		set_temp_variable = { GXC_stability_loss_temp_var = GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_stability_loss_temp_var = -0.25 } #Between -0.25 to 0.00
		add_stability = GXC_stability_loss_temp_var

		set_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = GXC_party_pop_diff_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = -200 } #Between -200 to 0.00
		add_political_power = GXC_pp_loss_temp_var

		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = CHN_deduct_stab_and_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_tt
			IDEOLOGY = social_conservative_coloured
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			#Rig it if you have game rules
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_HANMIN_DIARCHY_AUTDEM }
				}
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.514 days = 14 } #Revenge of the Cantonese
			}
			#Normal Pathing
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat > party_popularity@social_conservative } }
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.514 days = 14 } #Revenge of the Cantonese
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.513 days = 14 } #The Western Hills Strikes Back
			}
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_or_potential_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.516 days = 1 random_days = 2 } #A Last Gasp of Civilian Rule
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_HANMIN_DIARCHY_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_KMT_path option = GXC_KMT_PATH_PATAUT }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_game_rule_rigged_warning_tt
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Yue-Gui Face-off
	id = GXC.lategame.505
	title = GXC.lategame.505.t
	desc = GXC.lategame.505.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_KMT_NRA_soldier_flag

	is_triggered_only = yes #Event: GXC.lategame.500
	timeout_days = 10 #To Ensure its done in time for the big vote

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.505 option GXC.lategame.505.a"
		name = GXC.lategame.505.a #We will throw our support behind Li Zongren's candidacy!
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		add_political_power = -25
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC = { country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.506 days = 1 } } #[FROM.GetNLameDefCap] Supports Li Zongren
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.505 option GXC.lategame.505.b"
		name = GXC.lategame.505.b #We shall endorse Ju Zheng for national leadership!
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		add_political_power = -25
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC = { country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.507 days = 1 } } #[FROM.GetNameDefCap] Endorses Ju Zheng
		}
	}
	option = {

		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.505 option GXC.lategame.505.e"
		name = GXC.lategame.505.e #[FROM.GetName] Denounces Yue-Gui

			limit = { china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes } #PREV is GXC

			add_stability = -0.10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes } #LKMT or Republicans
			add_political_power = -50
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			#Everyone else
			add_political_power = -30
			add_stability = -0.03

		CHN_add_to_civil_war_preparation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC = { country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.509 days = 1 } } #[FROM.GetNameDefCap] Stand For Themselves!
		}
	}

country_event = { #The Republic Teeters to the Brink
	id = GXC.lategame.515
	title = GXC.lategame.515.t
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.515.d.yunkmt
		trigger = {
			tag = YUN
			china_alignment_right_kuomintang = yes
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.515.d.shxgmj
		trigger = {
			tag = SHX
			has_country_leader = {
				character = SHX_feng_yuxiang
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.515.d.shxyan
		trigger = {
			tag = SHX
			has_country_leader = {
				character = SHX_yan_xishan
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.515.d.generic
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_NRA_soldiers_4

	is_triggered_only = yes #Event: GXC.lategame.504.a

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.515 option GXC.lategame.515.a"
		name = GXC.lategame.515.a #If we stand for nothing, what'll we fall for?
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GXC
					ratio > 0.80
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				ic_ratio = {
					tag = GXC
					ratio > 0.8
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				GXC = { has_war = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_chinese_tag = no
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GXC
					ratio < 0.75
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				check_variable = { CHN_civil_war_preparation_var > 0 }
			}
		}
		#Penalty depending on your alignment - PP and Stab already deducted earlier.
		if = {
			limit = { china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes } #PREV is GXC
			add_command_power = -100
			add_war_support = -0.10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes } #LKMT or Republicans
			add_command_power = -50
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			#Everyone else
			add_command_power = -30
			add_war_support = -0.03
		}

		#Break the Puppetship
		china_break_puppet_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FROM
				type = topple_government
			}
		}

		#Inform GXC
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = YUN }
				country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.550 days = 0 } #Advance of the National Protectors
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.445 days = 1 } #[FROM.GetLeader] Contests the Election!
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.515 option GXC.lategame.515.b"
		name = GXC.lategame.515.b #Dying is easy, living is harder.
		trigger = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = no }
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		add_political_power = 15
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.515 option GXC.lategame.515.c"
		name = GXC.lategame.515.c #It is time we bring our province into the fold.
		trigger = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				OR = {
					china_alignment_left_kuomintang = yes
					has_country_leader = { character = SHX_feng_yuxiang }
					has_country_leader = { character = HNN_tan_yankai }
				}
			}
		}

		effect_tooltip = { china_integrate_ally_effect = yes }

		GXC = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_done_our_patriotic_duty_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC = {
				country_event = { id = china_events.18 days = 3 } #[FROM.Adjective] Nationalists Return to the Fold
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	desc = GXC.lategame.605.d

		name = GXC.lategame.605.a #After discussions, the gentlemen agreed to call for a national general election.
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_power_balance_in_range = {
					id = UPC_power_balance
					range > UPC_bop_developing_realism
				}
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_FIRST_SOCDEM }
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_SECOND_SOCDEM }
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_SECOND_SOCLIB }
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_FIRST_SOCLIB }
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_YE_JU_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_power_balance_in_range = {
					id = UPC_power_balance
					range > UPC_bop_emerging_idealism
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_GXC_UPC_PATH_JISHEN_TUTELAGE_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_JISHEN_RENAISSANCE_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_QIYOU_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_GXC_UPC_PATH_YE_JU_PATAUT }
				}
			}
		}

		GXC_DSP_medium_effect = yes
		GXC_PIP_medium_effect = yes
		UPC_add_enthusiasm_large_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_power_balance_in_range = {
						id = UPC_power_balance
						range < UPC_bop_growing_idealism
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_UPC_lategame_dem_enthusiam_too_high_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_FIRST_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_SECOND_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_SECOND_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_FIRST_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_YE_JU_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_game_rule_rigged_warning_tt
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.630 days = 1 } #The [GetYear] Chinese Federal Elections
			if = {
				limit = { has_war = yes }
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.606 days = 14 } #A Wartime Political Truce
			}
		}
	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.605 option GXC.lategame.605.b"
		name = GXC.lategame.605.b #The two men settle on an assembly vote and a renewed unity government.
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_power_balance_in_range = {
					id = UPC_power_balance
					range < UPC_bop_growing_idealism
				}
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_GXC_UPC_PATH_JISHEN_TUTELAGE_AUTDEM }
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_JISHEN_RENAISSANCE_AUTDEM }
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_QIYOU_AUTDEM }
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_GXC_UPC_PATH_YE_JU_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_FIRST_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_SECOND_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_SECOND_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_FIRST_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_YE_JU_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		GXC_YUE_large_effect = yes
		UPC_sub_enthusiasm_large_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_power_balance_in_range = {
						id = UPC_power_balance
						range > UPC_bop_developing_realism
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_UPC_lategame_dem_enthusiam_too_low_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_GXC_UPC_PATH_JISHEN_TUTELAGE_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_JISHEN_RENAISSANCE_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_UPC_PATH_QIYOU_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_UPC_path option = GXC_GXC_UPC_PATH_YE_JU_PATAUT }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_game_rule_rigged_warning_tt
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.660 days = 3 } #The National Unity Cabinet
		}
	}
}
