### NPA Satellite Events (900-929):
country_event = {
	id = GXC.lategame.900 #The Sino-Japanese War Begins
	title = GXC.lategame.900.t
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.900.d.chen
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_chen_lianbo_favored_flag
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_chen_lianbo_favored_flag
						has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag
					}
					NOT = { paternal_autocrat > party_popularity@social_conservative }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.900.d.shen
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_chen_lianbo_favored_flag
						has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag
					}
					paternal_autocrat > party_popularity@social_conservative
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_HNN_new_army_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes #Fired 3 days after [EVENT]: ai_events.205 The SSJW War Event.
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#If you haven't set a favored side, set it now.
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_chen_lianbo_favored_flag
						has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { paternal_autocrat > party_popularity@social_conservative }
					set_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag
				}
				else = {
					set_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_chen_lianbo_favored_flag
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.900 option GXC.lategame.900.a"
		name = GXC.lategame.900.a #A plot brews in the East.
		#Lategame Debuffs and Phase IV Flag delayed until one side wins.
		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC.lategame.900.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			overlord = { country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.901 days = 3 } } #Telegram from Guangzhou
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = GXC.lategame.901 #Telegram from Guangzhou
	title = GXC.lategame.901.t
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.901.d.chen
		trigger = {
			GXC = { NOT = { has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag } }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.901.d.shen
		trigger = {
			GXC = { has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_guangzhou_government_gate

	is_triggered_only = yes #Fired 3 days after [EVENT]: GXC.lategame.900

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.901 option GXC.lategame.901.a"
		name = GXC.lategame.901.a #We will lend our support to Guangdong.
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		if = {
			limit = { GXC = { has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag } }
			#For every non-Pat Aut party popularity in GXC, costs 1pp (max 100).
			set_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = 1 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = GXC.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
			multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = -100 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = CHN_deduct_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_in_country_tt
				IDEOLOGY = paternal_autocrat_coloured COUNTRY = "[GXC.GetNameDef]"
			}
			add_political_power = GXC_pp_loss_temp_var
			custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_NPA_shen_hongying_warning_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_NPA_guranteed_shen_coup_warning_tt
		}
		else = {
			#For every non-Rad Soc party popularity in GXC, costs 1pp (max 100).
			set_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = 1 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = GXC.party_popularity@social_conservative }
			multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = -100 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = CHN_deduct_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_in_country_tt
				IDEOLOGY = social_conservative_coloured COUNTRY = "[GXC.GetNameDef]"
			}
			add_political_power = GXC_pp_loss_temp_var
			custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_NPA_chen_lianbo_warning_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_NPA_guranteed_chen_coup_warning_tt
		}

		GXC = { save_event_target_as = GXC_NPA_overlord_backs_guangdong_coup }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.901 option GXC.lategame.901.b"
		name = GXC.lategame.901.b #We will stay silent on this matter.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						GXC = { has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag }
						check_variable = { GXC.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat > 0.5 }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { GXC = { has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag } }
						check_variable = { GXC.party_popularity@social_conservative > 0.5 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_NPA_lu_yuguang_warning_tt
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC = { country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.902 days = 3 } } #The Guangdong Coup
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = GXC.lategame.902 #The Guangdong Coup
	title = GXC.lategame.902.t
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.902.d.chen
		trigger = {
			GXC = { NOT = { has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag } }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.lategame.902.d.shen
		trigger = {
			GXC = { has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_guangxi_troops_3

	is_triggered_only = yes #Fired 3 days after [EVENT]: GXC.lategame.901

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GXC_phase_4_begins_flag
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			#Devastation effects since we're in phase IV
			CHN_setup_lategame_debuffs_effect = yes
			GXC_clear_phase2_debuffs = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.902 option GXC.lategame.902.a"
		name = GXC.lategame.902.a #The coup succeeds and drives back the Guangxi counter-attack.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					AND = {
						GXC = { has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag }
						check_variable = { GXC.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat > 0.35 }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { GXC = { has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag } }
						check_variable = { GXC.party_popularity@social_conservative > 0.35 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = { CHN_setup_lategame_debuffs_effect = yes }
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		#Inform the player if they are forced into a coup because their popularity is too high.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag
				paternal_autocrat > 0.50
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_NPA_guranteed_shen_coup_warning_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag }
				social_conservative > 0.50
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_NPA_guranteed_chen_coup_warning_tt
		}

		#Deduct any PP
		if = {
			limit = { GXC = { has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag } }
			#For every non-Pat Aut party popularity in GXC, costs 1pp (max 100).
			set_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = 1 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = GXC.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
			multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = -100 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = CHN_deduct_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_in_country_tt
				IDEOLOGY = paternal_autocrat_coloured COUNTRY = "[GXC.GetNameDef]"
			}
			add_political_power = GXC_pp_loss_temp_var

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no #No new elections until post unification tree
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				promote_character = {
					character = GXC_shen_hongying
					ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
				}
				activate_advisor = GXC_zhu_jiahua_sic
				news_event = { id = GXC.lategame.904 days = 1 } #Shen Hongying's Coup in Guangdong
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.940 days = 320 random_days = 80 } #The Rise of Zhu Jiahua
			}
		}
		else = {
			#For every non-Soc Con party popularity in GXC, costs 1pp (max 100).
			set_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = 1 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = GXC.party_popularity@social_conservative }
			multiply_temp_variable = { GXC_pp_loss_temp_var = -100 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = CHN_deduct_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_in_country_tt
				IDEOLOGY = social_conservative_coloured COUNTRY = "[GXC.GetNameDef]"
			}
			add_political_power = GXC_pp_loss_temp_var

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_conservative
				elections_allowed = no #No new elections until post unification tree
			}
			set_capital = {
				state = 592 #Guangzhou
				remember_old_capital = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				promote_character = {
					character = GXC_chen_lianbo
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
				}
				GXC_chen_gongshou = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
				activate_advisor = GXC_chen_gongshou_sic
				news_event = { id = GXC.lategame.903 days = 1 } #Chen Lianbo's Coup in Guangdong
				country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.930 days = 320 random_days = 80 } #Liu Zhenhuan Seizes Guangxi
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.lategame.902 option GXC.lategame.902.b"
		name = GXC.lategame.902.b #The coup fails after a decisive Guangxi counter-attack.
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag
					paternal_autocrat > 0.50
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = GXC_NPA_satellite_shen_hongying_favored_flag }
					social_conservative > 0.50
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		effect_tooltip = { CHN_setup_lategame_debuffs_effect = yes }
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		#Punish Players for going against master's wishes
		if = {
			limit = { has_event_target = GXC_NPA_overlord_backs_guangdong_coup }
			add_stability = -0.20
			add_war_support = -0.20
			custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_NPA_going_against_masters_wishes_tt
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FROM
				modifier = KR_outraged
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -0.10
			add_war_support = -0.10
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = no #No new elections until post unification tree
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = {
				character = GXC_lu_yuguang
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			activate_advisor = GXC_ma_ji_sic
			news_event = { id = GXC.lategame.905 days = 1 } #Marshal Lu Fends off the Guangdong Coup
			country_event = { id = GXC.lategame.950 days = 320 random_days = 80 } #The Marshal and His Men
		}
	}

	after = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = focus_tree_will_change_tt
	}
}

country_event = { #The Hour of Federal Democracy?
	id = GXC.endgame.300
	title = GXC.endgame.300.t
	desc = GXC.endgame.300.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_federalist_party_3

	is_triggered_only = yes #Fired by [DECISION] china_declare_unification

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GXC_phase_5_begins_flag
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes

			country_event = { id = GXC.endgame.301 days = 3 }
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_or_potential_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = GXC.endgame.310 days = 5 } #Dawn of a Federal Democracy?
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #And so concludes the Zeitgest of the 1920s.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.300 option GXC.endgame.300.a"
		name = GXC.endgame.300.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_subject = no }
				news_event = china_events.358 #Guangdong's Federalists Unite China
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				ic_ratio = {
					tag = GXC
					ratio > 0.8
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				GXC = { has_war = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_chinese_tag = no
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GXC
					ratio < 0.75
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				check_variable = { CHN_civil_war_preparation_var > 0 }
			}
		}
		#Penalty depending on your alignment - PP and Stab already deducted earlier.
		if = {
			limit = { china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes } #PREV is GXC
			add_command_power = -100
			add_war_support = -0.10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes } #Republicans
			add_command_power = -50
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			#Everyone else
			add_command_power = -30
			add_war_support = -0.03
		}

		#Break the Puppetship
		china_break_puppet_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FROM
				type = topple_government
			}
		}

		#Inform GXC
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = YUN }
				country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.760 days = 0 } #The Nation's Call
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = GXC.endgame.311 days = 1 } #The [FROM.Adjective] Rebellion
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.310 option GXC.endgame.310.b"
		name = GXC.endgame.310.b #We welcome President [UPC.GetLeader]!
		trigger = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = no }
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		add_political_power = 15
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.310 option GXC.endgame.310.c"
		name = GXC.endgame.310.c #Let us send a delegation to the capital. (Switch to [UPC.GetNameDef])
		trigger = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { character = SHX_feng_yuxiang }
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = { china_integrate_ally_effect = yes }
		GXC = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_done_our_patriotic_duty_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC = {
				country_event = { id = china_events.190 days = 3 } #[FROM.Adjective] Federalists Join Our Government
			}
		}
	}
}

###Dem Back Sliding Events (430-459):
country_event = { #The Fall of the Chen/Zhang Government
	id = GXC.endgame.430
	title = {
		text = GXC.endgame.430.t.zhang
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { character = GXC_zhang_junmai }
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = GXC.endgame.430.t.chen
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = GXC_zhang_junmai } }
		}
	}
	desc = GXC.endgame.430.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_ye_ju_1

	is_triggered_only = yes #Fired by [BOP] UPC_bop_emerging_realism OR UPC_bop_bitter_realism

	option = { #Democracy in our federation has taken a mighty blow...
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.430 option GXC.endgame.430.a"
		name = GXC.endgame.430.a
		UPC_sub_enthusiasm_mega_effect = yes
		UPC_end_federalist_democracy_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = UPC_new_national_elections
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = yes #So natural pace of elections will still happen and you get the auth dem elections event.
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no #No new elections until post unification tree
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = {
				character = GXC_ye_ju
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			activate_advisor = GXC_ma_yuhang_sic

			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = GXC_UPC_popular_support_the_party_of_washington }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GXC_UPC_popular_support_the_party_of_washington
					add_idea = GXC_UPC_popular_support_5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = GXC_UPC_popular_support_republic_of_yin_and_yang }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GXC_UPC_popular_support_republic_of_yin_and_yang
					add_idea = GXC_UPC_popular_support_5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = GXC_UPC_popular_support_socialism_of_all_mankind }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GXC_UPC_popular_support_socialism_of_all_mankind
					add_idea = GXC_UPC_popular_support_5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = GXC_UPC_popular_support_democracy_by_decree }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GXC_UPC_popular_support_democracy_by_decree
					add_idea = GXC_UPC_popular_support_5
				}
			}
			#Uncomplete focuses
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GXC_reorganising_the_dsp
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = GXC_reorganising_the_dsp
					uncomplete_children = yes
					refund_political_power = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GXC_a_multi_partisan_democracy
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = GXC_a_multi_partisan_democracy
					uncomplete_children = yes
					refund_political_power = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GXC_pursuing_a_federal_democracy
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = GXC_pursuing_a_federal_democracy
					uncomplete_children = yes
					refund_political_power = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Li Jishen's Coup
	id = GXC.endgame.511
	title = GXC.endgame.511.t
	desc = GXC.endgame.511.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_li_jishen_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes #Fired by [EVENT] GXC.endgame.510.

	option = { #Is this a new Bonaparte?
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.511 option GXC.endgame.511.a"
		name = GXC.endgame.511.a
		CHI_li_jishen = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
				promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						desc = CHI_li_jishen_leader_desc
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
						traits = { CHN_federalist_aligned }
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = GXC_NRG_party_long_tt
				name = GXC_NRG_party
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		UPC_sub_enthusiasm_mega_effect = yes
		activate_advisor = GXC_assorted_leaders_sic
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		GXC_chen_jiongming = { retire = yes }
		GXC_chen_qiyou = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = social_liberal_subtype }
				promote_character = social_liberal_subtype
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						desc = GXC_chen_qiyou_leader_desc
						ideology = social_liberal_subtype
						traits = { CHN_federalist_aligned }
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		GXC_purge_the_yue_clique = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = GXC_NRG_party_long
				name = GXC_NRG_party
			}
			CHI_li_jishen = { china_set_character_alignment_federalists = yes }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Nanning Insurrection
	id = GXC.endgame.520
	title = GXC.endgame.520.t
	desc = {
		text = GXC.endgame.520.d.yunfed
		trigger = {
			tag = YUN
			china_alignment_federalists = yes
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.endgame.520.d.hnnfed
		trigger = {
			tag = HNN
			china_alignment_federalists = yes
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.endgame.520.d.szcfed
		trigger = {
			tag = SZC
			china_alignment_federalists = yes
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.endgame.520.d.generic
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					china_alignment_federalists = yes
					OR = {
						tag = YUN
						tag = HNN
						tag = SZC
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_zhili_battle

	is_triggered_only = yes #[EVENT] GXC.endgame.504

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.520 option GXC.endgame.520.a"
		name = GXC.endgame.520.a #We have made our bed, now lie in it. (Switch to [UPC.GetNameDef])
		trigger = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				OR = {
					china_alignment_left_kuomintang = yes
					has_country_leader = { character = SHX_feng_yuxiang }
					has_country_leader = { character = YUN_tang_jiyao }
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = { china_integrate_ally_effect = yes }
		GXC = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_done_our_patriotic_duty_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC = {
				country_event = { id = china_events.190 days = 3 } #[FROM.Adjective] Federalists Join Our Government
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.520 option GXC.endgame.520.b"
		name = GXC.endgame.520.b #Perhaps it is time to wait-and-see?
		trigger = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = no }
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		add_political_power = 15
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.520 option GXC.endgame.520.c"
		name = GXC.endgame.520.c #They have shown the folly of their ways! At arms!
		trigger = {
			CHN_has_civil_war_prep_trigger = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GXC
					ratio > 0.80
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				ic_ratio = {
					tag = GXC
					ratio > 0.8
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				GXC = { has_war = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_chinese_tag = no
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GXC
					ratio < 0.75
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				check_variable = { CHN_civil_war_preparation_var > 0 }
			}
		}
		#Penalty depending on your alignment - PP and Stab already deducted earlier.
		if = {
			limit = { china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes } #PREV is GXC
			add_command_power = -100
			add_war_support = -0.10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes } #Republicans
			add_command_power = -50
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			#Everyone else
			add_command_power = -30
			add_war_support = -0.03
		}

		#Break the Puppetship
		china_break_puppet_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FROM
				type = topple_government
			}
		}

		#Inform GXC
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = YUN }
				country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.760 days = 0 } #The Nation's Call
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = GXC.endgame.311 days = 1 } #The [FROM.Adjective] Rebellion
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #A New Age Under Liangguang
	id = GXC.endgame.600
	title = GXC.endgame.600.t
	desc = GXC.endgame.600.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_beijing_beiyang_flag

	is_triggered_only = yes #Fired by [DECISION] china_declare_unification

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GXC_phase_5_begins_flag
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			country_event = { id = GXC.endgame.601 days = 3 }
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_or_potential_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = GXC.endgame.610 days = 5 } #The NPA Dissolves
			}
			CHI = {
				CHI_wang_jingwei = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
				CHI_chen_duxiu = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			}

			#Organize Endgame Parties
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				long_name = CHN_radicals_party_long
				name = CHN_radicals_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = GXC_assorted_leaders
				ideology = totalist_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				long_name = CHN_CSP_party_long
				name = CHN_CSP_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = CHI_chen_duxiu
				ideology = syndicalist_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = CHN_KMT_party_long
				name = CHN_KMT_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = CHI_wang_jingwei
				ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = CHN_FCDP_party_long #Includes DCP so that frees up Auth Dem for Republicans
				name = CHN_FCDP_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = GXC_zhang_junmai
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = CHN_GRA_party_long
				name = CHN_GRA_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = GXC_chen_jiongming
				ideology = social_liberal_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				long_name = GXC_psc_party_national_long
				name = GXC_psc_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = GXC_liu_zhenhuan
				ideology = market_liberal_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				long_name = CHN_YCP_party_long
				name = CHN_YCP_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = GXC_zhang_zizhu
				ideology = national_populist_subtype
			}

			#Okay Path Specific Now
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = { character = GXC_chen_lianbo }
						has_country_leader = { character = GXC_liu_zhenhuan }
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					long_name = GXC_aacsc_party_long
					name = GXC_aacsc_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = GXC_chen_lianbo
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					long_name = CHN_republicans_party_long
					name = CHN_republicans_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = GXC_assorted_leaders
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					long_name = CHN_regionalists_party_long
					name = CHN_regionalists_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = GXC_assorted_leaders
					ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = { character = GXC_shen_hongying }
						has_country_leader = { character = GXC_zhu_jiahua }
						has_country_leader = { character = GXC_li_yaohan }
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					long_name = CHN_republicans_party_long
					name = CHN_republicans_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = GXC_assorted_leaders
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					long_name = GXC_JXS_party_long
					name = GXC_JXS_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = GXC_zhu_jiahua
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				}
				#May switch to national variant in a later event.
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					long_name = GXC_ogxc_saf_party_long
					name = GXC_ogxc_saf_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = GXC_shen_hongying
					ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					long_name = CHN_republicans_party_long
					name = CHN_republicans_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = GXC_assorted_leaders
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
				}
				#May switch in a later event.
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					long_name = GXC_ogxc_ygf_national_party_long
					name = GXC_ogxc_ygf_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = GXC_lu_yuguang
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					long_name = CHN_regionalists_party_long
					name = CHN_regionalists_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = GXC_assorted_leaders
					ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Unification, if we can keep it.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.600 option GXC.endgame.600.a"
		name = GXC.endgame.600.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_subject = no }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_leader = { character = GXC_chen_lianbo } }
					news_event = china_events.362 #Cantonese Merchants Unite China
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_leader = { character = GXC_lu_yuguang } }
					news_event = china_events.361 #Guangxi Warlords Unite China
				}
				else = {
					news_event = china_events.3610 #Guangxi Warlords Unite China (Shen)
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The NPA dissolves
	id = GXC.endgame.610
	title = GXC.endgame.610.t
	desc = {
		text = GXC.endgame.610.d.yunlong
		trigger = {
			tag = YUN
			has_country_leader = { character = YUN_long_yun }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.endgame.610.d.yunhu
		trigger = {
			tag = YUN
			has_country_leader = { character = YUN_hu_ruoyu }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.endgame.610.d.shxyan
		trigger = {
			tag = SHX
			has_country_leader = {
				character = SHX_yan_xishan
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.endgame.610.d.generic
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = YUN
				tag = SHX
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_warlord_observer

	is_triggered_only = yes #Event: GXC.endgame.434.c

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.610 option GXC.endgame.610.a"
		name = GXC.endgame.610.a #This is our moment, and we will take it!

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GXC
					ratio > 0.80
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				ic_ratio = {
					tag = GXC
					ratio > 0.8
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				GXC = { has_war = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_chinese_tag = no
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GXC
					ratio < 0.75
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				check_variable = { CHN_civil_war_preparation_var > 0 }
			}
		}

		#No need for penalty depending on alignment since this an NPA tag. will do baseline penalty.
		add_command_power = -30
		add_war_support = -0.03

		#Break the Puppetship
		china_break_puppet_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FROM
				type = topple_government
			}
		}

		#Inform GXC
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = GXC.endgame.611 days = 1 } #An Alliance in Tatters
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.610 option GXC.endgame.610.b"
		name = GXC.endgame.610.b #We willingly go from allies to subjects...for now at least.
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		add_political_power = 15
	}
}

			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					tag = SHX
					tag = YUN
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_warlord_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes #Event: GXC.endgame.610

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.611 option GXC.endgame.611.a"
		name = GXC.endgame.611.a #There is but one fate for rebels!
		trigger = { tag = GXC }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FROM
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.611 option GXC.endgame.611.b"
		name = GXC.endgame.611.b #There can only be one master of China."
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = GXC } }
	}
}

country_event = { #To Rule a Nation
	id = GXC.endgame.630
	title = GXC.endgame.630.t
	desc = GXC.endgame.630.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_ma_junwu

	is_triggered_only = yes #Fired 3 days after [FOCUS] The Young Face of An Ancient Nation

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#In case this didn't happen already
			GXC_lu_yuguang = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			GXC_ma_junwu = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			GXC_ma_ji = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
		}
	}

	option = { #General Ma Ji is a natural fit for the job.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.630 option GXC.endgame.630.a"
		name = GXC.endgame.630.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 65

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_NPA_path option = GXC_NPA_PATH_YUGUANG_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			save_current_party_popularities = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GXC_new_authdem_value = saved_popularities^8 } #Current Pat Aut
			set_temp_variable = { GXC_new_pataut_value = saved_popularities^7 } #Current Auth Dem
			set_popularities = {
				totalist = saved_popularities^0
				syndicalist = saved_popularities^1
				radical_socialist = saved_popularities^2
				social_democrat = saved_popularities^3
				social_liberal = saved_popularities^4
				market_liberal = saved_popularities^5
				social_conservative = saved_popularities^6
				authoritarian_democrat = GXC_new_authdem_value
				paternal_autocrat = GXC_new_pataut_value
				national_populist = saved_popularities^9
			}

			#May switch in a later event.
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = CHN_regionalists_party_long
				name = CHN_regionalists_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = GXC_assorted_leaders
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = GXC_ogxc_ygf_national_party_long
				name = GXC_ogxc_ygf_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = GXC_lu_yuguang
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			}
			activate_advisor = GXC_ma_ji_sic
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GXC.endgame.630.a_tt
		set_politics = { ruling_party = paternal_autocrat }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.10
		}
	}
	option = { #Scholar Ma Junwu will be Prime Minister.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event GXC.endgame.630 option GXC.endgame.630.b"
		name = GXC.endgame.630.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GXC_NPA_path option = GXC_NPA_PATH_YUGUANG_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = {
				character = GXC_lu_yuguang
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			activate_advisor = GXC_ma_junwu_sic
		}
	}
}

	}

		text = GXC.endgame.900.d.PAC
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = { character = CHI_song_qingling }

			}
		}
	}
	desc = {

		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { character = CHI_hu_zongnan }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = GXC.endgame.900.d.RKMT

				tag = RKT

				has_country_leader = { character = HNN_tang_shengzhi }

		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_propaganda_kmt_parade
